/JS/General/APPRequest.asp?id=35638986&src=JobApply&pgid=657218852566480192&red=/JS/General/Job.asp?id=35638986~amp~a=apply~amp~src=JobApply :: 127 :: Updated: 8/21/2011 :: 128 :: <STRONG> Program/Project Manager </STRONG> :: 129 :: <BR/> :: 130 :: A Program/Project Manager is responsible for the full end-to-end delivery of business solutions to the business. A Program/Project Manager is a hands-on expert in project planning and execution including: scope definition and managements, task and resource scheduling, cost and price budgeting, quality review and assurance, client relationship management, project team management, and overall change management. The Program/Project Manager will be 100% accountable for the on-time, on budget delivery of solutions per the approved specifications. :: 131 :: <BR/> :: 132 :: <BR/> :: 133 :: This resource will manage all phases of the Software Development Lifecycle, from initial ideation phases to the final project closure activities. To be successful, this resource must be detailed oriented and willing to dive into the details of a project to flush out issues and risks, while simultaneously possessing the ability to see the bigger picture and understand the interdependencies of the overall program. A Program/Project Manager will be responsible for large complex projects that span organizations, geographies, and technologies, often with direct accountability to Executive Management. This resource must have excellent leadership skills and must be able to work with a diverse project team consisting of resources from all parts of the organization (both IT & Business). :: 134 :: <BR/> :: 135 :: <BR/> :: 136 :: The Program/Project Manager will likely be responsible for either a) a portfolio of projects that together achieve a common business goal and objective, or b) a single large project or program that consists of multiple phases of both IT and Business components. :: 137 :: <BR/> :: 138 :: <BR/> :: 139 :: The Program/Project Manager will be a strategic thinking, quality driven individual, who will provide leadership, direction, coordination and coaching for project managers and project teams during their day to day management and implementation of IT & Business projects, programs, activities and processes. :: 140 :: <BR/> :: 141 :: <BR/> :: 142 :: <BR/> :: 143 :: Requirements: :: 144 :: <BR/> :: 145 :: <BR/> :: 146 :: Maintains overall accountability for the successful delivery of the designated project / program to the Business. :: 147 :: <BR/> :: 148 :: <BR/> :: 149 :: Establishes work plan tracking procedures, status reporting, issue management, change management, resource management, configuration management, financial management, etc. :: 150 :: <BR/> :: 151 :: <BR/> :: 152 :: Coordinates, directs and monitors IT & Business programs ensuring consistency of processes across projects :: 153 :: <BR/> :: 154 :: <BR/> :: 155 :: Communicates with program/project managers and solution managers to ensure projects adhere to all phases of software development lifecycle management :: 156 :: <BR/> :: 157 :: <BR/> :: 158 :: Ensures that all ongoing projects are run within the constraints of scope, quality, time and cost :: 159 :: <BR/> :: 160 :: <BR/> :: 161 :: Conducts and supports training programs for the program/project managers and teams :: 162 :: <BR/> :: 163 :: <BR/> :: 164 :: Creates reports and documentation to measure status of projects and review results on a weekly, monthly and quarterly basis :: 165 :: <BR/> :: 166 :: <BR/> :: 167 :: Manages 3rd party vendors selected to participate in assigned projects, including full vendor management procedures. :: 168 :: <BR/> :: 169 :: <BR/> :: 170 :: Performs analysis of program/project issues, resolves problems, identifies and recommends improvement opportunities as related to the policies of the PMO. Participates in PMO functions, processes, and rollout. :: 171 :: <BR/> :: 172 :: <BR/> :: 173 :: Facilitates the detailed definition and scoping of projects including both the IT portions of a project and the Business / Business process components of the project. :: 174 :: <BR/> :: 175 :: <BR/> :: 176 :: Prepares estimates and develops project plans. :: 177 :: <BR/> :: 178 :: <BR/> :: 179 :: Coordinates with both Business Unit resources as well as IT resources. :: 180 :: <BR/> :: 181 :: <BR/> :: 182 :: Manages communication between internal customers and various functional groups :: 183 :: <BR/> :: 184 :: <BR/> :: 185 :: Provides technical consultation to other IT groups. :: 186 :: <BR/> :: 187 :: <BR/> :: 188 :: Participates in vendor evaluations and provides recommendations. :: 189 :: <BR/> :: 190 :: <BR/> :: 191 :: Improves quality results by implementing unit, system and integration testing cycles. :: 192 :: <BR/> :: 193 :: <BR/> :: 194 :: Understands and uses critical path management. :: 195 :: <BR/> :: 196 :: <BR/> :: 197 :: Proactively identifies and communicates risks to project development and schedule. :: 198 :: <BR/> :: 199 :: <BR/> :: 200 :: Monitors and drives resolution of issues. :: 201 :: <BR/> :: 202 :: <BR/> :: 203 :: Adheres to clients Governance, PM methods, and tools/templates as appropriate. :: 204 :: <BR/> :: 205 :: <BR/> :: 206 :: - Prior Tier 1 Consulting Experience preferred :: 207 :: <BR/> :: 208 :: - 12+ years of total work experience preferred :: 209 :: <BR/> :: 210 :: - 7+ years of PM experience required :: 211 :: <BR/> :: 212 :: - 2+ :: 114 :: 	<BR/> :: 115 :: 	Job Number: :: 116 :: 	<B> 35498701 </B> :: 117 :: 	Company Name: :: 118 :: 	<B> Liberty Mutual Group </B> :: 119 :: 	Job Location: :: 120 :: 	<B> Dover, NH US </B> :: 121 :: Job Categories: :: 122 :: <B> Insurance </B> :: 123 :: <BR/> :: 124 :: <B> Information Technology </B> :: 125 :: More Information :: 126 :: Javascript:; :: 127 :: Updated: 7/27/2011 :: 128 :: <STRONG> Project Leader - Dover, NH </STRONG> :: 129 :: <BR/> :: 130 :: About Liberty Mutual Group Helping people live safer, more secure lives since 1912, Boston-based Liberty Mutual Group is a diversified global insurer and third largest property and casualty insurer in the U.S. based on A.M. Best Company's report of 2010 net written premium. The Group also ranks 82nd on the Fortune 100 list of largest corporations in the U.S. based on 2010 revenue. As of December 31, 2010, Liberty Mutual Group had $112.4 billion in consolidated assets, $95.4 billion in consolidated liabilities, and $33.2 billion in annual consolidated revenue. Liberty Mutual Group offers a wide range of insurance products and services, including personal automobile, homeowners, workers compensation, property, commercial automobile, general liability, global specialty, group disability, reinsurance and surety. Liberty Mutual Group (www.libertymutualgroup.com) employs over 45,000 people in more than 900 offices throughout the world. :: 131 :: <BR/> :: 132 :: <BR/> :: 133 :: Advance your career at Liberty Mutual - A Fortune 100 Company! :: 134 :: <BR/> :: 135 :: As the Project Leader you will serve as the business owner of Life company Architecture and agent portal and be responsible for leading the development and implementation of a highly visible state-of-the-art portal. You will be a hands-on business leader tasked with developing and progressing online suite of tools provided to the sales staff and the customers by establishing more robust digital capabilities to accelerate customer acquisition, broaden the Company's online capabilities and deepen customer relationships. The Project Leader manages all aspects of complex Departmental or Division projects. Negotiates project objectives and direction with senior managers. Projects vary in scope and duration :: 136 :: <BR/> :: 137 :: Responsibilities: :: 138 :: <BR/> :: 139 :: * Implement business vision and roadmap for Individual Life Architecture and agent portal capabilities. :: 140 :: <BR/> :: 141 :: * Works with technology project managers on business requirements, functional design, prototyping, process design (including scenario design, flow mapping), testing, training, defining support procedures and supporting implementations for an integrated portal platform; oversees implementation and manages continual system improvements. :: 142 :: <BR/> :: 143 :: * Translates Web Department/Division needs into a comprehensive project plan which ensures successful project completion. :: 144 :: <BR/> :: 145 :: * Conceptualizes immediate and long-range analytical needs of the lines of business. :: 112 :: 	<BR/> :: 113 :: 	Job Number: :: 114 :: 	<B> 35106623 </B> :: 115 :: 	Company Name: :: 116 :: 	<B> Macy's </B> :: 117 :: 	Job Location: :: 118 :: 	<B> Plymouth Meeting, PA US </B> :: 119 :: Job Categories: :: 120 :: <B> Sales & Sales Management </B> :: 121 :: <BR/> :: 122 :: <B> Customer Service </B> :: 123 :: More Information :: 124 :: Javascript:; :: 125 :: Updated: 7/19/2011 :: 126 :: <STRONG> Macy's Philadelphia Area: Sales Manager & Sales Supervisor Opportunities </STRONG> :: 127 :: <BR/> :: 128 :: Interested in a career with Macy's? :: 129 :: Macy's is looking for top talent candidates for entry level Store Management opportunities. Potential opportunities include Sales Supervisor or Sales Manager position. :: 130 :: As a Sales Manager or a Sales Supervisor, you will support My Macy's by driving sales and selling with focus on the Macy's customer. All activities related to presenting a clean, neat and organized shopping environment for our customers are under your direction. With training, coaching and development, a team of Associates will grow following your leadership. :: 131 :: <STRONG> Key Accountabilities: </STRONG> :: 132 :: <BR/> :: 133 :: <BR/> :: 134 :: <STRONG> Sales </STRONG> :: 135 :: Drive and exceed sales goals by executing Macy's initiatives :: 136 :: Lead the push toward selling through coaching and recognition :: 137 :: Review and utilize reports; implement action plans focusing on deficient areas :: 138 :: Identify best sellers and key items; communicate merchandise needs to optimize the My Macy's process :: 139 :: Ensure accuracy of promotional presentation; communicate advertising and sales information to Associates :: 140 :: Partner with Merchandising team to plan and execute floor moves, merchandise placement and sales set-up :: 141 :: Review your personal Selling Area Scorecard monthly for your Associate Turnover, Sales & Star Rewards results :: 142 :: Strengthen attendance and weekend hours compliance among staff :: 143 :: Motivate Associates to solicit our Star Rewards Program by reinforcing the benefits of new accounts :: 144 :: Establish high level of shortage awareness and effectiveness; ensure that all policies and procedures are implemented :: 145 :: <STRONG> Customer </STRONG> :: 146 :: Coach Associates to consistently deliver effective selling behaviors resulting in high customer engagement :: 147 :: Review & utilize Associate Scorecards to provide recognition; develop and communicate strategies to improve results :: 148 :: Observe Associates twice daily through formal observations focusing on selling behaviors; ensure Associates are providing an outstanding shopping experience to all customers :: 149 :: Coach to Associate Scorecard metrics weekly through daily informal observations defining one focus metric and behaviors to improve an individual metric :: 150 :: Ensure optimum sales floor coverage and lead selling initiatives throughout the store as needed :: 151 :: Maintain high customer readiness standards; deliver a clean, neat and easy to shop store environment :: 152 :: <STRONG> People </STRONG> :: 153 :: Recruit a qualified team of selling-focused Associates; build a bench for future advancements & promotions :: 154 :: Ensure all Associate training is conducted on a timely basis, ensure assigned mentors engage with new hires :: 155 :: Coach Associates on product knowledge by holding in-store product training with Vendor Representatives :: 156 :: Actively fill open positions prioritizing internal Associates in Commission, Specialist and High Level selling areas :: 157 :: Engage in Macy's recognition program; reward Associates with recognition cards :: 158 :: Meet with Associates in department weekly; identify top sellers and talk about opportunities :: 159 :: Conduct ongoing Talent Analysis of Associates and establish career progression plans for key players and positions to result in retention of best people and turnover reduction :: 160 :: Utilize review process as a tool for Associate talent development, promotion and advancement :: 161 :: Monitor and address performance issues on a timely basis :: 162 :: Address Associate concerns in a reasonable and fair manner, consistent with the values expected by the Company :: 163 :: Lead team to support giving back to the local community helping create stronger, healthier places to live and work :: 164 :: <STRONG> Skills Summary: </STRONG> :: 165 :: <BR/> :: 166 :: A minimum of 1-3 years in a leadership/supervisory position in a service-driven environment :: 167 :: Ability to empower and develop a team :: 168 :: Ability to collaborate and function as a member of a team :: 169 :: Ability to execute plans and strategies :: 170 :: Strong leadership, interpersonal and communication skills :: 171 :: Highly organized and able to adapt quickly to changing priorities :: 172 :: Ability to anticipate and solve problems, act decisively and persist in the face of obstacles :: 173 :: Commitment to exemplifying the highest integrity and professional business standards :: 174 :: <STRONG> Macy's is an Equal Opportunity Employer, committed to a diverse and inclusive work environment. </STRONG> :: 112 :: 	<BR/> :: 113 :: 	Job Number: :: 114 :: 	<B> 35174769 </B> :: 115 :: 	Company Name: :: 116 :: 	<B> Bank of America </B> :: 117 :: 	Job Location: :: 118 :: 	<B> Wayne, PA US </B> :: 119 :: Job Category: :: 120 :: <B> Accounting & Finance </B> :: 121 :: More Information :: 122 :: Javascript:; :: 123 :: Updated: 7/21/2011 :: 124 :: <STRONG> Financial Advisor Trainee - Wayne, PA </STRONG> :: 125 :: <BR/> :: 126 :: The Practice Management Development (PMD) role is a training program to develop and prepare future Financial Advisors for a successful new career. The primary focus of the PMD role is to build and enhance client relationships under close supervision of coaches and managers. These client relationships are the base for your book of business. Financial Advisor Trainees learn to assess client needs, meet with existing and prospective clients, review investment goals and prepare recommendations for products such as stocks, bonds, options, mutual funds and annuities. :: 127 :: We are currently accepting resumes for the following offices: Wayne, PA :: 128 :: <BR/> :: 129 :: <B> The Financial Advisor Trainee engages in: </B> :: 130 :: <BR/> :: 131 :: Developing a book of business in order to meet and exceed the required performance hurdles :: 132 :: Effectively sourcing prospective clients, capitalizing on referrals, assessing customer needs, referring customers to the appropriate service provider, and executing highly customized solutions to meet the customer needs :: 133 :: Recommending investment products and services that are suitable for prospects and clients based on their objectives, resources, time horizon, risk profile and preferences :: 134 :: Balancing investment growth, referral activities, customer follow up, prospect building, administrative compliance and personal growth and development according to both a day-to-day and longer-term plan :: 135 :: Planning and managing resources (time, people, budget) to run a productive practice :: 136 :: Seeking the expertise of specialists, where appropriate, to identify planning and investment strategies for a client :: 137 :: Establishing and maintaining relationship with the management team and informing management of any circumstances that require supervisory attention/review/approval as per compliance guidelines and policies :: 138 :: Completing mandated training, assessments, performance goals and continuing education requirements :: 139 :: <BR/> :: 140 :: <B> The Financial Advisor Trainee receives: </B> :: 141 :: <BR/> :: 142 :: The strength and name recognition of Merrill Lynch and Bank of America. :: 143 :: A base salary through the full three plus years in the PMD program. This roll will become a fully commissioned position after completion of the PMD program. :: 144 :: World class training throughout their career with Merrill Lynch :: 145 :: State of the art software programs to assist in your success :: 146 :: Access to a full array of investment and banking products for your clients :: 147 :: Coaches or mentors located within your office to work with you towards your success :: 148 :: <BR/> :: 149 :: <B> Ideal candidates: </B> :: 150 :: <BR/> :: 151 :: The PMD program is designed for individuals ready to make a career transition and follow their passion of becoming a Financial Advisor. Successful candidates have at least three years of full time sales experience in ever more challenging environments. The sales experience should include the successful use of outbound sales techniques to exceed sales goals. Financial acumen gained through work experience is ideal. :: 152 :: <B> Essential Duties and Responsibilities </B> :: 153 :: : :: 154 :: Performance Hurdles: A Financial Advisor Trainee must acquire clients through personalized marketing techniques to meet minimum performance hurdles. :: 155 :: Registration and Licensing Requirement: A Financial Advisor Trainee is required to obtain necessary licensing and registrations (Series 7 and Series 66 and Insurance). :: 156 :: Education Requirement: A Financial Advisor Trainee is required to complete the Certified Financial Planner (CFP) Investment Planning Course and the Financial Planning course . :: 157 :: Development Assessment: A Financial Advisor Trainee must successfully complete ongoing Developmental Assessments throughout the training. In preparation for the assessment, the Financial Advisor Trainee studies a variety of topics and may participate in developmental activities in the areas including but not limited to: Merrill Lynch strategy, products & services, wealth management process, desk top technology, marketing consultative sales skills and investment financial planning knowledge :: 158 :: Performance Requirements: A Financial Advisor Trainee is expected to meet the performance and development requirements of the PMD Program and transition to a full Financial Advisor at the conclusion of the PMD Program. :: 159 :: <BR/> :: 160 :: <B> Qualifications: </B> :: 161 :: <BR/> :: 162 :: Qualifications: Must possess 3 or more years of sales experience with a proven record of exceeding goals Outbound sales experiences required Possess excellent communication skills, both written and verbal Proven relationship building and business partnering skills Passion to grow your current financial knowledge to share with others Candidate must be self-motivated and proactive Bachelors degree or higher strongly preferredIndustry Experience: Active Series 6 or Series 7 license preferred 6 months in a Series 6 or 7 sales role preferred Proven successful financial product sales experience preferred Strong financial acumen required Track record of success Clean U-4 and U-5 history, if licensedProfessional designations/licenses: Candidates may apply without Series 7, 66 and insurance licenses, but must achieve all required licenses within 13 weeks of accepting this position.Merrill Lynch is an Equal <STRONG> Macy's Philadelphia Area: Sales Manager & Sales Supervisor Opportunities </STRONG> :: 127 :: <BR/> :: 128 :: Interested in a career with Macy's? :: 129 :: Macy's is looking for top talent candidates for entry level Store Management opportunities. Potential opportunities include Sales Supervisor or Sales Manager position. :: 130 :: As a Sales Manager or a Sales Supervisor, you will support My Macy's by driving sales and selling with focus on the Macy's customer. All activities related to presenting a clean, neat and organized shopping environment for our customers are under your direction. With training, coaching and development, a team of Associates will grow following your leadership. :: 131 :: <STRONG> Key Accountabilities: </STRONG> :: 132 :: <BR/> :: 133 :: <BR/> :: 134 :: <STRONG> Sales </STRONG> :: 135 :: Drive and exceed sales goals by executing Macy's initiatives :: 136 :: Lead the push toward selling through coaching and recognition :: 137 :: Review and utilize reports; implement action plans focusing on deficient areas :: 138 :: Identify best sellers and key items; communicate merchandise needs to optimize the My Macy's process :: 139 :: Ensure accuracy of promotional presentation; communicate advertising and sales information to Associates :: 140 :: Partner with Merchandising team to plan and execute floor moves, merchandise placement and sales set-up :: 141 :: Review your personal Selling Area Scorecard monthly for your Associate Turnover, Sales & Star Rewards results :: 142 :: Strengthen attendance and weekend hours compliance among staff :: 143 :: Motivate Associates to solicit our Star Rewards Program by reinforcing the benefits of new accounts :: 144 :: Establish high level of shortage awareness and effectiveness; ensure that all policies and procedures are implemented :: 145 :: <STRONG> Customer </STRONG> :: 146 :: Coach Associates to consistently deliver effective selling behaviors resulting in high customer engagement :: 147 :: Review & utilize Associate Scorecards to provide recognition; develop and communicate strategies to improve results :: 148 :: Observe Associates twice daily through formal observations focusing on selling behaviors; ensure Associates are providing an outstanding shopping experience to all customers :: 149 :: Coach to Associate Scorecard metrics weekly through daily informal observations defining one focus metric and behaviors to improve an individual metric :: 150 :: Ensure optimum sales floor coverage and lead selling initiatives throughout the store as needed :: 151 :: Maintain high customer readiness standards; deliver a clean, neat and easy to shop store environment :: 152 :: <STRONG> People </STRONG> :: 153 :: Recruit a qualified team of selling-focused Associates; build a bench for future advancements & promotions :: 154 :: Ensure all Associate training is conducted on a timely basis, ensure assigned mentors engage with new hires :: 155 :: Coach Associates on product knowledge by holding in-store product training with Vendor Representatives :: 156 :: Actively fill open positions prioritizing internal Associates in Commission, Specialist and High Level selling areas :: 157 :: Engage in Macy's recognition program; reward Associates with recognition cards :: 158 :: Meet with Associates in department weekly; identify top sellers and talk about opportunities :: 159 :: Conduct ongoing Talent Analysis of Associates and establish career progression plans for key players and positions to result in retention of best people and turnover reduction :: 160 :: Utilize review process as a tool for Associate talent development, promotion and advancement :: 161 :: Monitor and address performance issues on a timely basis :: 162 :: Address Associate concerns in a reasonable and fair manner, consistent with the values expected by the Company :: 163 :: Lead team to support giving back to the local community helping create stronger, healthier places to live and work :: 164 :: <STRONG> Skills Summary: </STRONG> :: 165 :: <BR/> :: 166 :: A minimum of 1-3 years in a leadership/supervisory position in a service-driven environment :: 167 :: Ability to empower and develop a team :: 168 :: Ability to collaborate and function as a member of a team :: 169 :: Ability to execute plans and strategies :: 170 :: Strong leadership, interpersonal and communication skills :: 171 :: Highly organized and able to adapt quickly to changing priorities :: 172 :: Ability to anticipate and solve problems, act decisively and persist in the face of obstacles :: 173 :: Commitment to exemplifying the highest integrity and professional business standards :: 174 :: <STRONG> Macy's is an Equal Opportunity Employer, committed to a diverse and inclusive work environment. </STRONG> <STRONG> Macy's NJ South Area: Sales Manager & Sales Supervisor Opportunities </STRONG> :: 127 :: <BR/> :: 128 :: Interested in a career with Macy's? :: 129 :: Macy's is looking for top talent candidates for entry level Store Management opportunities. Potential opportunities include Sales Supervisor or Sales Manager position. :: 130 :: As a Sales Manager or a Sales Supervisor, you will support My Macy's by driving sales and selling with focus on the Macy's customer. All activities related to presenting a clean, neat and organized shopping environment for our customers are under your direction. With training, coaching and development, a team of Associates will grow following your leadership. :: 131 :: <STRONG> Key Accountabilities: </STRONG> :: 132 :: <BR/> :: 133 :: <BR/> :: 134 :: <STRONG> Sales </STRONG> :: 135 :: Drive and exceed sales goals by executing Macy's initiatives :: 136 :: Lead the push toward selling through coaching and recognition :: 137 :: Review and utilize reports; implement action plans focusing on deficient areas :: 138 :: Identify best sellers and key items; communicate merchandise needs to optimize the My Macy's process :: 139 :: Ensure accuracy of promotional presentation; communicate advertising and sales information to Associates :: 140 :: Partner with Merchandising team to plan and execute floor moves, merchandise placement and sales set-up :: 141 :: Review your personal Selling Area Scorecard monthly for your Associate Turnover, Sales & Star Rewards results :: 142 :: Strengthen attendance and weekend hours compliance among staff :: 143 :: Motivate Associates to solicit our Star Rewards Program by reinforcing the benefits of new accounts :: 144 :: Establish high level of shortage awareness and effectiveness; ensure that all policies and procedures are implemented :: 145 :: <STRONG> Customer </STRONG> :: 146 :: Coach Associates to consistently deliver effective selling behaviors resulting in high customer engagement :: 147 :: Review & utilize Associate Scorecards to provide recognition; develop and communicate strategies to improve results :: 148 :: Observe Associates twice daily through formal observations focusing on selling behaviors; ensure Associates are providing an outstanding shopping experience to all customers :: 149 :: Coach to Associate Scorecard metrics weekly through daily informal observations defining one focus metric and behaviors to improve an individual metric :: 150 :: Ensure optimum sales floor coverage and lead selling initiatives throughout the store as needed :: 151 :: Maintain high customer readiness standards; deliver a clean, neat and easy to shop store environment :: 152 :: <STRONG> People </STRONG> :: 153 :: Recruit a qualified team of selling-focused Associates; build a bench for future advancements & promotions :: 154 :: Ensure all Associate training is conducted on a timely basis, ensure assigned mentors engage with new hires :: 155 :: Coach Associates on product knowledge by holding in-store product training with Vendor Representatives :: 156 :: Actively fill open positions prioritizing internal Associates in Commission, Specialist and High Level selling areas :: 157 :: Engage in Macy's recognition program; reward Associates with recognition cards :: 158 :: Meet with Associates in department weekly; identify top sellers and talk about opportunities :: 159 :: Conduct ongoing Talent Analysis of Associates and establish career progression plans for key players and positions to result in retention of best people and turnover reduction :: 160 :: Utilize review process as a tool for Associate talent development, promotion and advancement :: 161 :: Monitor and address performance issues on a timely basis :: 162 :: Address Associate concerns in a reasonable and fair manner, consistent with the values expected by the Company :: 163 :: Lead team to support giving back to the local community helping create stronger, healthier places to live and work :: 164 :: <STRONG> Skills Summary: </STRONG> :: 165 :: <BR/> :: 166 :: A minimum of 1-3 years in a leadership/supervisory position in a service-driven environment :: 167 :: Ability to empower and develop a team :: 168 :: Ability to collaborate and function as a member of a team :: 169 :: Ability to execute plans and strategies :: 170 :: Strong leadership, interpersonal and communication skills :: 171 :: Highly organized and able to adapt quickly to changing priorities :: 172 :: Ability to anticipate and solve problems, act decisively and persist in the face of obstacles :: 173 :: Commitment to exemplifying the highest integrity and professional business standards :: 174 :: <STRONG> Macy's is an Equal Opportunity Employer, committed to a diverse and inclusive work environment. </STRONG> Large pharmaceutical company in north central New Jersey is seeking a Procurement Manager for HR Services and HR Operations. The position will support the Global Category Leader for the HR Services Categories, in sub categories including HR Operations, HR Administration, Outplacement, Background Screening, Relocation and others as required. Develop and implement sourcing strategies to support the direction set by the senior leadership, global category leader and key stakeholders.Â Maintain a global perspective on the category by coordinating implementation details with regional sourcing contacts. Develop and maintain strong relationships with internal stakeholders in order to understand their business drivers and support them/those requirements from a Procurement perspective. Also, develop and maintain relationships with key suppliers, share new industry knowledge and administer a supplier performance management program. Study industry trends in order to understand their impacts on the category. :: 133 :: Qualifications include:Â Bachelorâ€™s Degree with MBA preferred, or minimum 6-10 years procurement experience preferably gained in a similarly diverse and operationally complex environment. :: 127 :: Updated: 7/28/2011 :: 128 :: <STRONG> Human Resources Generalist </STRONG> :: 129 :: <BR/> :: 130 :: <B> Job Description </B> :: 131 :: <B> Title: Human Resources Generalist </B> :: 132 :: <B> About Iron Mountain </B> :: 133 :: <BR/> :: 134 :: Iron Mountain Incorporated (NYSE: IRM) provides information management services that help organizations lower the costs, risks and inefficiencies of managing their physical and digital data. The company's solutions enable customers to protect and better use their information—regardless of its format, location or lifecycle stage—so they can optimize their business and ensure proper recovery, compliance and discovery. Founded in 1951, Iron Mountain manages billions of information assets, including business records, electronic files, medical data, emails and more for organizations around the world. Visit :: 135 :: www.ironmountain.com :: 136 :: http://www.ironmountain.com/ :: 137 :: or follow the company on Twitter at :: 138 :: www.twitter.com/IronMountainInc :: 139 :: http://www.twitter.com/IronMountainInc :: 140 :: for more information. :: 141 :: We are currently recruiting for a Human Resources Generalist. :: 142 :: Job Summary :: 143 :: <BR/> :: 144 :: Performs Human Resources related duties at the professional level. Functional areas of responsibility will include employee relations, training, employment, labor relations, affirmative action and employment equity programs. This position will typically support a single territory within NAO. :: 145 :: <BR/> :: 146 :: Essential Functions :: 147 :: Partners with employees and management to communicate various Human Resources policies, procedures, laws, standards and government regulations. :: 148 :: Conducts exit interviews, analyzes data, and makes recommendations to the management team for corrective action and continuous improvement. :: 149 :: Responds to employee relations issues such as employee complaints, harassment allegations, and civil rights complaints. :: 150 :: Facilitates and/or provides training to the workforce. Training sessions to include hourly harassment and workplace violence training as well as exempt Human Resource introductory training. :: 151 :: Interviews, screens, and recruits job applicants to fill entry level, professional and technical job openings. :: 152 :: Reviews applications and interviews applicants to match experience with specific job related requirements. :: 153 :: Maintains working relationship with Union officials and adheres to terms of labor contract by monitoring day-to-day implementation of policies concerning wages, hours and working conditions. (as needed) :: 154 :: Represents management in investigating, answering, and settling grievances, by arranging and scheduling grievance hearings between union personnel, supervisor and the Management team. (as needed) :: 155 :: Assists HR Manager in responding to outside agency charges :: 156 :: Participate in HR task forces and corporate project teams :: 157 :: Partners with compensation to conduct and implement salary surveys :: 158 :: Attends market leadership meetings :: 159 :: Organize and participate in employee roundtable meetings :: 160 :: Conduct formal HR visits to assigned markets utilizing appropriate documentation :: 161 :: Job Requirements :: 162 :: KNOWLEDGE, SKILLS, AND ABILITIES :: 163 :: Pertinent federal, state and local laws, regulations and codes :: 164 :: Principles and practices of recruitment and selection :: 165 :: Techniques for dealing with a variety of individuals from various socio- economic, ethnic and cultural backgrounds :: 166 :: Ability to objectively coach employees and management through routine employee relations matters :: 167 :: The ability to research and analyze Human Resources data. :: 168 :: Make recommendations to effective resolve problems or issues, by using judgment that is in consistent with standards, practices, policies, procedures, regulation or government law :: 169 :: Ability to organize and prioritize work :: 170 :: Ability to work in a matrix environment :: 171 :: Ability to engage in limited overnight travel :: 172 :: Bachelor's degree Human Resources Management, or a related field :: 173 :: One to two years experience in Human Resources Management :: 174 :: Background in employment law and other government compliance regulations is preferred :: 175 :: <BR/> :: 176 :: <BR/> :: 177 :: The ideal applicant will have current exp. in Human Resources. :: 178 :: <BR/> :: 179 :: <BR/> :: 180 :: At this time we are considering only local candidates who are able to work without employer sponsorship. No agencies or phone calls, please. :: 181 :: <BR/> :: 182 :: Only those candidates whose experience best meets our requirements will be contacted. :: 183 :: Iron Mountain is an Equal Opportunity <STRONG> Teller Operations Specialist - Western NJ - Rocky Hill - 40 Hours </STRONG> :: 129 :: <BR/> :: 130 :: <STRONG> Responsibilities: </STRONG> :: 131 :: Teller Operations Specialists are primarily responsible for driving day-to-day operational excellence and ensuring compliance requirements are met. Your duties will include, but are not limited to the following: :: 132 :: Coach and train the teller team to process transactions accurately, efficiently in accordance with established policies and procedures. :: 133 :: Create a positive team environment in the banking center by modeling appropriate behaviors. :: 134 :: Assist teller associates by using in-depth policy and procedure knowledge to handle more complex transactions and issues. :: 135 :: Maintain the highest level of customer service standards while consistently delighting our customers and exceeding expectations. :: 136 :: Ensure banking center compliance is within federal regulations. :: 137 :: Work closely and provide input to the Banking Center Manager and Assistant Manager to continually improve banking center performance. :: 138 :: Create workforce stability by cultivating an engaged, spirited and well-coached team. :: 139 :: Process transactions accurately and efficiently to build customer confidence and trust, based on established policies and procedures. :: 140 :: May be required to work Saturdays and or extended hours as needed. :: 141 :: <BR/> :: 142 :: <B> Qualifications: </B> :: 143 :: <BR/> :: 144 :: <STRONG> Required Skills </STRONG> :: 145 :: : :: 146 :: Minimum two years cash handling experience :: 147 :: Minimum two years customer service experience :: 148 :: Minimum one year coaching/leadership/management experience within past 3 years :: 149 :: Effectively lead team to performance goals :: 150 :: Direct and motivate staff :: 151 :: Excellent oral and written communication skills :: 152 :: Extensive experience in assisting customers with inquires and/or problem resolution :: 153 :: Identifying opportunities to enhance customer financial needs, goals and objectives :: 154 :: Heightened attention to detail, time management and organization :: 155 :: Advanced computer skills :: 156 :: <STRONG> Desired Skills/Assets </STRONG> :: 157 :: : :: 158 :: Ability to manage retail operations, as well as plan goals, schedules and objectives and conduct audits :: 159 :: Successful cross-selling experience :: 160 :: Previous banking/financial <STRONG> AVP, Associate Administrative Manager (Hopewell, NJ/Charlotte, NC/Lincoln, RI/Jax, FL) </STRONG> :: 127 :: <BR/> :: 128 :: The Associate Administrative Manager position will serve to ensure regulatory compliance and corporate mandates for all administrative and operational activities performed in the Merrill Edge Self Directed platform. A predominate objective of the position is to limit risk and financial exposure to the business unit and the firm. :: 129 :: Responsibilities include (but are not limited to) the following: :: 130 :: New Account Approval :: 131 :: Conduct supervisory reviews including RMS, EOD & OTR. :: 132 :: Cash to Margin review :: 133 :: Approving market action trade corrections and review/audit monthly error logs :: 134 :: Review and maintain all Compliance and Regulatory Correspondence including email and Fax2mail :: 135 :: Monitor accounts with large debit balances and short market values over $500,000 and coordinate approval with Credit Administration and clients :: 136 :: <BR/> :: 137 :: <B> Qualifications: </B> :: 138 :: <BR/> :: 139 :: Series 7, 63/65 or 66, 8 or 9/10 (or FINRA equivalent 4,24,53) required to be considered for the role :: 140 :: Strong Leadership and Communication skills :: 141 :: Merrill Edge self directed, MEAC or Branch Office CA, FA or Operations experience :: 142 :: Familiarity with compliance and regulatory issues :: 143 :: <BR/> :: 144 :: <B> Other Locations: </B> :: 145 :: US-NC-Charlotte, US-FL-Jacksonville, US-RI-Lincoln :: 146 :: <BR/> :: 147 :: <B> :: 129 :: Updated: 7/28/2011 :: 130 :: <STRONG> Assistant General Manager Distribution Center (Cranbury NJ) </STRONG> :: 131 :: <BR/> :: 132 :: POSITION PURPOSE :: 133 :: <BR/> :: 134 :: <BR/> :: 135 :: The DC Assistant General Manager is responsible for the success of all operational functions within the highly complex distribution center environment of approximately 500,000 + square feet to ensure that it is an outstanding place to work. The DC Assistant General Manager is responsible for the supervision of a large team of DC Operations Managers in the Inbound, Warehouse, Outbound and Office Operations. The DC AGM works with the General Manager to develop strategies and objectives to maximize productivity and leverage expenses for the Home Depot distribution center. They must also be capable of working with Associates, Department Supervisors, DC Operations Managers, the General Manager as well as Stores, third party vendors, and the Merchandising, Supply Chain and Operations functions. :: 136 :: <BR/> :: 137 :: <BR/> :: 138 :: MAJOR TASKS, RESPONSIBILITIES AND KEY ACCOUNTABILITIES :: 139 :: <BR/> :: 140 :: <BR/> :: 141 :: Assists General Managers with the evaluation of the effectiveness of and recommends alternatives for work methods, procedures, controls and staffing to achieve accurate and timely movement and processing of product; leading associates to anticipate and solve problems and plan for upcoming events, seasonal changes, etc. to ensure warehouse layout is optimally aligned for maximum efficiency as seasonality and inventory needs require. :: 142 :: <BR/> :: 143 :: <BR/> :: 144 :: Provides recommendations to General Managers with the DC's financial, operational, people and process and service related objectives to drive continuous improvement and efficiency gains to reduce overall cost-to-serve; leads associates, and peers to anticipate and solve problems and plan for upcoming events, seasonal changes, etc. Depending on DC, may lead management of 3PL provider to ensure optimal performance and metrics are achieved. :: 145 :: <BR/> :: 146 :: <BR/> :: 147 :: Leads to ensure operational excellence in all warehouse areas, efficient operations of warehouse management system(s) and related equipment, inventory is received appropriately and efficiently and safely processed in the warehouse, proper layout of warehouse and product placement, and proper maintenance and organization of all warehouse areas so that it's appearance is conducive to creating a perfect load for our Stores and Customers :: 148 :: <BR/> :: 149 :: <BR/> :: 150 :: Coaches, trains, and develops management team informally and through formal training programs, providing both informal (e.g. on-floor coaching) and formal (e.g. written evaluation) job performance based feedback. Maintains a union free work environment by creating an employee-centered work place that demonstrates care and concern for all Associates. :: 151 :: <BR/> :: 152 :: <BR/> :: 153 :: Ensure a culture of safety throughout the organization by following Home Depot safety policies and procedures - monitor DC safety, physical security and operational metrics on a daily, weekly and monthly basis :: 154 :: <BR/> :: 155 :: <BR/> :: 156 :: NATURE AND SCOPE :: 157 :: <BR/> :: 158 :: <BR/> :: 159 :: Reports to DC General Manager - II :: 160 :: <BR/> :: 161 :: <BR/> :: 162 :: Accountable for the management of a department or functional group through subordinate supervisors/managers and for all personnel issues -- including selection, termination, performance appraisal and professional development of subordinates. :: 163 :: <BR/> :: 164 :: <BR/> :: 165 :: ENVIRONMENTAL JOB REQUIREMENTS :: 166 :: <BR/> :: 167 :: <BR/> :: 168 :: ESSENTIAL SKILLS :: 169 :: <BR/> :: 170 :: <BR/> :: 171 :: MINIMUM QUALIFICATIONS :: 172 :: <BR/> :: 173 :: <BR/> :: 174 :: Must be eighteen years of age :: 175 :: <BR/> :: 176 :: <BR/> :: 177 :: Must pass the Drug Test :: 178 :: <BR/> :: 179 :: <BR/> :: 180 :: Must pass the Background Check :: 181 :: <BR/> :: 182 :: <BR/> :: 183 :: Must pass pre-employment tests if applicable :: 184 :: <BR/> :: 185 :: <BR/> :: 186 :: EDUCATION REQUIRED :: 187 :: <BR/> :: 188 :: <BR/> :: 189 :: The knowledge, skills and abilities typically acquired through the completion of a high school diplomas and/or GED. :: 190 :: <BR/> :: 191 :: <BR/> :: 192 :: YEARS OF RELEVANT WORK EXPERIENCE - 3 :: 193 :: <BR/> :: 194 :: <BR/> :: 195 :: PHYSICAL JOB REQUIREMENTS :: 196 :: <BR/> :: 197 :: <BR/> :: 198 :: Requires intermittent periods during which continuous physical exertion is required, such as walking, standing, stooping, climbing, lifting material or equipment, some of which may be heavy or awkward. :: 199 :: <BR/> :: 200 :: <BR/> :: 201 :: ADDITIONAL QUALIFICATIONS :: 202 :: <BR/> :: 203 :: <BR/> :: 204 :: Ability to work a flexible schedule. Ability to be on-call at various times. Must be able to work weekends and holidays. :: 205 :: <BR/> :: 206 :: <BR/> :: 207 :: Must be open to relocation. 7/21/2011 :: 128 :: <STRONG> Senior Developer </STRONG> :: 129 :: <BR/> :: 130 :: Participates in design, development and implementation of systems engineering activities, to include OS technical support, systems programming and data center capabilities. Responsible for components of complex engineering and/or analytical tasks and activities. Assists in establishment of input/output processes and working parameters for hardware compatibility and coordination of subsystems design and integration of total system. Serves as a fully seasoned/proficient technical resource; provides tech knowledge and capabilities as team member and individual contributor. Will not have direct reports but will influence and direct activities of a team related to special initiatives or operations. Provides input on staffing, budget and personnel. Typically 5 or more years of systems engineering experience. :: 131 :: The senior developer position will be responsible for development various components of the appdashboard project and would participates in design activities. The senior developer will have at least 7 years of development experience with 5 years of development experience in JAVA. The senior developer should have experience in J2EE and J2SE development and be comfortable learning new technologies and languages at a fast-rate. The developer will need to be comfortable working in a fast-paced environment where requirements are fluid and quick turn-around is expected. Also requires ability to work with diverse groups :: 132 :: <BR/> :: 133 :: <B> Qualifications: </B> :: 134 :: <BR/> :: 135 :: Required Skills: :: 136 :: 7 years of development experience :: 137 :: * 128 :: NMS Labs is the nation’s leading independent provider of professional laboratory testing services, specializing in clinical toxicology, forensic science, and other vitally important areas of esoteric testing and expert services. We employ more than 200 highly trained professionals who work closely with leading healthcare providers, medical researchers and various members of the criminal and civil justice system to provide integrated testing and consultative services. :: 129 :: <BR/> :: 130 :: <BR/> :: 131 :: A job opening exists for a Systems Architect in our Information Technology department to design computer systems, administer databases, develop/enhance software, and implement commercial off the shelf software to support core organizational functions and assure their high availability. :: 132 :: <BR/> :: 133 :: <BR/> :: 134 :: * Develop solutions on technical platforms to support business processes and initiatives. Ability to design and develop highly complex programs. :: 135 :: <BR/> :: 136 :: * Work with operations teams and IT resources to understand enterprise architecture requirements and to align application and infrastructure specific goals. :: 137 :: <BR/> :: 138 :: * Provide technical leadership, from strategic decision making down to the project planning level. :: 139 :: <BR/> :: 140 :: * Ensure that information solutions are flexible to support incremental development, ongoing maintenance and future enhancements. Solutions need to ensure availability is maximized and support is simplified. :: 141 :: <BR/> :: 142 :: * Provide architectural expertise, direction, and assistance to other team members and software development teams. :: 143 :: <BR/> :: 144 :: * Confer with end-users, clients, or senior management to define business requirements for complex systems and infrastructure development. :: 145 :: <BR/> :: 146 :: * Conduct research on emerging technologies in support of systems development efforts, and recommend technologies that will increase cost effectiveness and systems flexibility. :: 147 :: <BR/> :: 148 :: * Presentation, analytical, and organizational skills are highly important, as well as, the ability to prepare and deliver informative presentations to varied audiences. :: 149 :: <BR/> :: 150 :: * Design long-term strategic goals and short-term tactical plans for technical architecture elements that support the business objectives. :: 151 :: <BR/> :: 152 :: * Make recommendations for the improvement and growth of the technology infrastructure. :: 153 :: <BR/> :: 154 :: * Manage projects. :: 155 :: <BR/> :: 156 :: * Work with the other administrators/analysts to ensure we have the tools and training for the new technologies. :: 157 :: <BR/> :: 158 :: <BR/> :: 159 :: Position requires a bachelor's degree in computer science (or chemistry, biology, or related analytical degree). Candidates must have 6 years of overall systems development lifecycle experience including 3 years of systems architecture experience. Experience working with .Net/C#, SQL, and/or Java programming. Experience with Oracle and SQL Server backup and recovery, database upgrades, and performance tuning. Experience with Windows operating systems is also required. A working knowledge of Laboratory Information Management Systems (LIMS), and enterprise reporting systems is a plus but not required. Demonstrated ability to multi-task, prioritize work, and communicate effectively is essential. Strong interpersonal skills required. :: 160 :: <BR/> :: 161 :: <BR/> :: 162 :: Located in suburban Philadelphia, NMS Labs offers a stimulating and diverse work environment with competitive salaries and great benefits, including medical/dental/prescription plan, life/STD/LTD, flexible spending account, tuition reimbursement, 401(k) plan with generous match, and a fully equipped fitness room. <STRONG> Macy's Suburban Square, Ardmore, PA: Retail Cosmetics Sales - Beauty Advisor, Part Time </STRONG> :: 127 :: <BR/> :: 128 :: <STRONG> Overview </STRONG> :: 129 :: <BR/> :: 130 :: We are currently seeking dynamic, self-motivated individuals who have a passion for cosmetics. The Cosmetic Department is one of the most vibrant, fast paced and exciting departments at Macy's. With extensive selling and product training, our Beauty Advisors practice superior selling techniques through advanced product knowledge and OUTSTANDING customer service. Our Beauty Advisors personally assist customers in makeup and skin care selections and participate in the execution of special events/promotions to achieve personal selling and service goals. As a Beauty Advisor you will be assigned to represent one of our prestigious cosmetics lines. currently seeking dynamic, self-motivated individuals who have a passion for cosmetics. With extensive selling and product training, our Beauty Advisors practice superior selling techniques through advanced product knowledge and OUTSTANDING customer service. Our Beauty Advisors personally assist customers in makeup and skin care selections and participate in the execution of special events/promotions to achieve personal selling and service goals. As a Beauty Advisor you will be assigned to represent one of our prestigious cosmetics lines.
